function info($str) { echo "INFO: $str\n"; }
function warn($str) { echo "WARNING: $str\n"; }
function err($str) { die("FATAL ERROR: $str\n"); }

@set_time_limit(0);

@header('Content-Type: text/plain');

chdir(__DIR__);
if (trim(@file_get_contents('oidplus_version.txt')) !== 'Revision 475') {
	err('This update can only be applied to OIDplus version 2.0.0.475!');
}

if (version_compare(PHP_VERSION, '7.0.0') < 0) {
	err('You need PHP Version 7.0 to update to this version');
}

// File added: res/.htaccess
function writefile_1() {
	@$fp = fopen('res/.htaccess', 'w');
	@fwrite($fp, base64_decode('T3JkZXIgRGVueSxBbGxvdwpEZW55IEZyb20gQWxsClJlcXVpcmUgYWxsIGRlbmllZAoK'));
	@fclose($fp);
}
if (is_file('res/.htaccess') && (sha1_file('res/.htaccess') != '6827a31b1ec7cc8d4e964e34f7ce5857b82a01ac')) {
	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: res/.htaccess');
	$tmp = pathinfo('res/.htaccess');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('res/.htaccess')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('res/.htaccess', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}
}
writefile_1();
if (!is_file('res/.htaccess')) {
	warn('File cannot be created (not existing): res/.htaccess');
} else if (sha1_file('res/.htaccess') != '6827a31b1ec7cc8d4e964e34f7ce5857b82a01ac') {
	warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): res/.htaccess');
} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('res/.htaccess', 0644)) {
	warn('Could not change file permissions of res/.htaccess');
}

if (!is_file('TODO')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: TODO');
	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('TODO')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): TODO');
	} else if (sha1_file('TODO') != '9aa75d23e9038fcfac1ebf3210f47f671eab660d') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): TODO');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('TODO', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of TODO');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '9aa75d23e9038fcfac1ebf3210f47f671eab660d') {
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'ebd45670f70b144825fdf2860688f6b070138990') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: TODO');
			$tmp = pathinfo('TODO');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('TODO')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('TODO', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '9aa75d23e9038fcfac1ebf3210f47f671eab660d') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): TODO');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('doc/install_iis.txt')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: doc/install_iis.txt');
	writefile_3();
	if (!is_file('doc/install_iis.txt')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): doc/install_iis.txt');
	} else if (sha1_file('doc/install_iis.txt') != '50481123d33a680d9953d8ee4deaa369ffa5c4f2') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): doc/install_iis.txt');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('doc/install_iis.txt', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of doc/install_iis.txt');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('doc/install_iis.txt') !== '50481123d33a680d9953d8ee4deaa369ffa5c4f2') {
		if (@sha1_file('doc/install_iis.txt') !== '8ae60904d986d24c6eaec1074e3ca918da39443c') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: doc/install_iis.txt');
			$tmp = pathinfo('doc/install_iis.txt');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('doc/install_iis.txt')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('doc/install_iis.txt', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('doc/install_iis.txt') !== '50481123d33a680d9953d8ee4deaa369ffa5c4f2') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): doc/install_iis.txt');
		}
	}
}

		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') != '939887ab2be661a1a46968f17addd4b330fb53a9') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	}

	if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '939887ab2be661a1a46968f17addd4b330fb53a9') {

			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');

			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_6();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '939887ab2be661a1a46968f17addd4b330fb53a9') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');

if (!is_file('setup/includes/setup_base.js')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: setup/includes/setup_base.js');
	writefile_9();
	if (!is_file('setup/includes/setup_base.js')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/includes/setup_base.js');
	} else if (sha1_file('setup/includes/setup_base.js') != '901420084d3e009a29395b93f34b6b38f3d88679') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/includes/setup_base.js');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/includes/setup_base.js', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/includes/setup_base.js');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('setup/includes/setup_base.js') !== '901420084d3e009a29395b93f34b6b38f3d88679') {
		if (@sha1_file('setup/includes/setup_base.js') !== '1c90dfcc1f5092ad97cb5bab455115a1c345215c') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/includes/setup_base.js');
			$tmp = pathinfo('setup/includes/setup_base.js');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/includes/setup_base.js')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('setup/includes/setup_base.js', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_9();
		if (@sha1_file('setup/includes/setup_base.js') !== '901420084d3e009a29395b93f34b6b38f3d88679') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/includes/setup_base.js');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('userdata/resources/info.txt')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: userdata/resources/info.txt');
	writefile_10();
	if (!is_file('userdata/resources/info.txt')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): userdata/resources/info.txt');
	} else if (sha1_file('userdata/resources/info.txt') != '4198c1386be784cf53786bc5b39618d186d41b42') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): userdata/resources/info.txt');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('userdata/resources/info.txt', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of userdata/resources/info.txt');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('userdata/resources/info.txt') !== '4198c1386be784cf53786bc5b39618d186d41b42') {
		if (@sha1_file('userdata/resources/info.txt') !== '2bc249fea07baaae7f4530e9e89b443e92b3263a') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: userdata/resources/info.txt');
			$tmp = pathinfo('userdata/resources/info.txt');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('userdata/resources/info.txt')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('userdata/resources/info.txt', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_10();
		if (@sha1_file('userdata/resources/info.txt') !== '4198c1386be784cf53786bc5b39618d186d41b42') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): userdata/resources/info.txt');
		}
	}
}

	@fwrite($fp, base64_decode('Pg0KCQkJCTwhLS0NCgkJCQlUbyAidW5sb2NrIiB0aGlzIHNlY3Rpb24sIHJ1biB0aGlzIGNvbW1hbmQ6DQoJCQkJJXdpbmRpciVcc3lzdGVtMzJcaW5ldHNydlxhcHBjbWQuZXhlIHVubG9jayBjb25maWcgLXNlY3Rpb246c3lzdGVtLndlYlNlcnZlci9zZWN1cml0'));

	@fclose($fp);
}
if (!is_file('web.config')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: web.config');
	writefile_11();
	if (!is_file('web.config')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): web.config');
	} else if (sha1_file('web.config') != '1aaa89a3b7c06e50a57dae4abfacbc6c3f14a0ae') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): web.config');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('web.config', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of web.config');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('web.config') !== '1aaa89a3b7c06e50a57dae4abfacbc6c3f14a0ae') {
		if (@sha1_file('web.config') !== 'cd93553f12e45e8126de0faff71ecb6758abf059') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: web.config');
			$tmp = pathinfo('web.config');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('web.config')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('web.config', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_11();
		if (@sha1_file('web.config') !== '1aaa89a3b7c06e50a57dae4abfacbc6c3f14a0ae') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): web.config');
		}
	}
}


file_put_contents('oidplus_version.txt', "Revision 476\n");
if (trim(@file_get_contents('oidplus_version.txt')) !== 'Revision 476') err('Could not write to oidplus_version.txt!');


echo 'DONE'; // This exact string will be compared in Update v3

@unlink(__FILE__);
if (is_file(__FILE__)) warn('Could not delete '.basename(__FILE__).'! Please delete it manually');
